1a1(1): dpal tshe bdag nag po'i phrin las kyi dgongs pa thams cad rdzogs pa'i rgyud chen po bzhugs so//
1b1(1): rgya gar skad du// thai ya yu ba ta~M kA la karmA sha ya sarba pAr+ha Na ma hA tan+ta/ bod skad du/ dpal tshe bdag nag po'i phrin las kyi dgongs pa thams cad rdzogs pa'i rgyud chen po//
1b2(1): bcom ldan 'das dpal tshe bdag nag po phrin las thams cad rdzogs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad lhun
1b3(1): gyis rdzogs pa'i rang bzhin rdo rje yongs su bkod pa'i snying po 'og min gyi gnas mkha' dbyings rnam par dag pa'i klong / rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa'i gzhal yas khang na/
1b4(1): 'khor rdo rje snying po nyid kyi rang bzhin dang dus gsum gcig pa'i sangs rgyas rnams dang / ma skyes pa'i lam la 'dun pa'i rig pa can rnams dang / sa la gnas pa'i byang chub
2a1(1): sems dpa' rnams dang / khro bo'i tshogs dregs pa can rnams dang / 'joms pa bdud kyi tshogs dang / khrag sdug ma mo'i tshogs dang / phreng byed mngag pa'i tshogs
2a2(1): dang / gdug pa gsum/ srin/ po'i tshogs dang thabs cig tu bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das la 'khor rnams kyis yongs su 'dun par gyur to// bcom ldan 'das
2a3(1): dpal rdo rje 'chang chen po des 'khor rnams yongs su 'dun par gzigs nas/ chos thams cad kun tu mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba'i snang bas khyab par mdzad do// de nas 'khor thams
2a4(1): cad sems 'grogs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis sems 'grogs par gzigs nas 'khor rnams la nyid kyi rang bzhin 'di bstan to// chos rnams ma skyes ye
2b1(1): nas gnyis su med// rgyu dang rkyen med rang byung gnas// de las kun 'byung rang byung thabs bsam yas// 'gro ba ma lus nga yi rang bzhin las// ma g.yo mi g.yo g.yo med cir yang gsal// snying po nyid
2b2(1): las g.yo ba ci yang med// ces gsungs so// de nas 'khor rnams kyis rang gi de nyid so so ma yin par rtogs par gyur to// de nas rdo rje snying po des// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang chen po la 'di skad ces
2b3(1): gsol to// kun gyi rang bzhin nyid lags par// gsang sngags ngo bo de kho na// dus gsum sangs rgyas nyid las med// nyid pas che ba rgyas par mdzod// ces gsol to// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang
2b4(1): chen po des// mi rtog pa rang byung gi dgongs pa chen po las 'od zer bye ba phrag sa ya phyogs bcur bkye'o// 'od zer des zhing khams thams cad du snang bas khyab par mdzad nas// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
2b5(1): dgongs pa brgyad de slar bsdus so// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rang bzhin/ chos thams cad kyi rtsa ba// rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid du mdzad nas sbyor ba'i don 'di nyid gsungs par gyur to// lhun gyis grub pa'i
2b6(1): gnas la gnas pa de// lus dbang sems yul 'dzin chags grol// kun gzhi nyid las bye brag gsum// rtsa ba gcig las lnga gnyis brgyad// bco brgyad bzhi dang ldan pa'i lha// tshe srog kun dbang gtso dang
3a1(1): 'bar// gnyis su med pa'i rang bzhin du// ston pas 'bras bu kun grub bshad// 'dab brgyad drangs ma bzhi dbus na// ston pa rang bzhin da 'khor rdzogs// rtag pa'i sgra lngam shes lnga/
3a2(1): lam 'khor lo rim brgyad gnas// lhun grub mchod pa rang gnas thim// rig pa'i ye shes rang las 'char// ston par 'bras bu gnyis 'grub bshad// yum gyi b+ha ga gsang ba'i gnas// rnam bzhi'i pho brang
3a3(1): lhun gyis grub// sgo khyams b+ha ga sna rtse la// yon tan lhun grub rin po che// rdo rje gsang ba'i lam sbyangs nas// ston pa'i gtso 'khor bstan pa'i dus// mnyam rdzogs gcig tu lhan cig skyes// bde ba'i
3a4(1): shes kun lam bcad// ston pas gsang ba'i sgo nas bcad// de nas bcom ldan 'das la rdo rje snying pos gsol pa// kye ho// rdo rje 'chang ba khro bo'i rgyal// rnam dag chos sgra'i rang bzhin las// 'gro ba 'dral
3a5(1): phyir sbrul skur bstan// 'khor gyi dregs pa pho mor bstan// dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs par mdzod// ces zhus so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis khro bo 'byung ba'i dgongs pa la bzhugs pas// 'jig
3a6(1): rten gsum po rab tu g.yos te/ ldeg rab tu ldeg cing kun tu ldeg/ 'ur 'ur rab tu 'ur 'ur kun tu 'ur ro// chem chem rab tu chem chem kun tu rab tu chem mo// mtha' mtho na dbus dma'/ dbus mtho na
3b1(1): mtha' dma' bar gyur to// 'jig rten gsum po 'jig la khang nas/ 'khor thams cad brgyal te lus sa la brdabs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis las thams cad yongs su rdzogs par gyur
3b2(1): pa'i phyir nga ro chen pos bsdigs so// he he e hur thums dza zhes bsgrags pas// 'jig rten gsum dang bcas pa'i srog 'phrog par gyur to// der phyogs bcu'i bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyang // 'khor
3b3(1): der skad cig ma gcig la lhags nas srog gi snying po thams cad mdongs gsol du phul lo// bcom ldan 'das kyis rngam pa'i sgra bton pas srog dang las thams cad 'dus par gyur to// A A A e ka zhes
3b4(1): rab tu brjod do// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang chen pos// 'khor rnams la gzigs te/ lhun gyis grub pa'i dkyil 'khor 'di gsungs so// rang bzhin mi gnas mnyam nyid las// lhun grub ye shes
3b5(1): gzhal yas khang // rin chen dur khrod brtan par gnas// phyi nang gnyis med brdal khyab gsal// gru bzhi sgo bzhi rta babs mdzes// rtse mo gnam lcags 'bar bcas mtho// lha brgyad klu brgyad zhing dang
3b6(1): ro// dra ba dra phyed zhing dang sbrul// glang chen 'brug dang seng ge stag/ rus sbal chu srin gnam lcags thog/ zhing dang zhing chung zod bu/ tsha pa/ khyung / kha khyer lha mo mchod sogs mdzes// e yi pho brang thod mkhar
4a1(1): bzhi// lcags mkhar bcu drug 'obs bcu gnyis// khyams dang gru chad sgo khyud ldan// rgyal chen pa yi pho brang na// klu 'bum gnyan khri sa bdag steng // phyogs skyong ma he nyi zla'i gdan// gzhan yang
4a2(1): zhing skyong nyi mar bcas// dbus na zil gnon lhun grub sku// mthing nag dug chen dug lnga 'joms// dbu gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhir bgrad// g.yas pa ku mu ta 'dra bas// ro nye za dang rngam par
4a3(1): gzigs// g.yon pa rA ga gnyen khri gsol// dbus mthing dgra bgegs don snying rol// 'khor lo ral gri rdo rje g.yas// be con gtun shing sdigs mdzub g.yon// glang chen la sogs dur khrod chas// rigs
4a4(1): bzhi rgyan dang rin po che// dbu la khrag 'thung lnga dang sbrul// klu brgyad mgo bcad do shal snying // gnod sbyin mgo bcad de bzhin dbu// bdud mo mthing nag thod sbrul 'khyud// ya ma dregs pa rus sbal
4a5(1): lhor// bya khyung spyi bo phrag sor khyung // stag dang seng ge sag nu ma// zhe sdang gdug pa sta zur gnyis/ khro chung phyi nang bar khyams gang // tsit+ta hUM zhes rtsa ba'i sngags// zod mkhar bla rkun mon pa bzhi// 'obs na
4a6(1): bdud pho bdud mo dang // mon pa rigs bzhi pho nya'i tshul// lcags mkhar sha za ki kang tshogs// gru chad sde brgyad dregs pa bcu/ khyams la 'chi bdag bdud kyi tshogs// mon pa mon mo rus sbal sbrul// mdun
4b1(1): na mgo dgu yab yum dang // srin mo lcags zag bla rkun dgu// lhun gyis grub pa'i phyag rgyar gsal// yongs su rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor du// gnyis med rig pa'i rang bzhin du// ston pas bca' gzhi
4b2(1): rdzogs par bshad// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das la rdo rje snying pos gsol pa/ sprul pa las kyi sbyor ba la// rnam grangs du dang ldan par byed// dgos pa'i rtog chen ci phyir 'brel// brnag pa'i mtha' ru gang
4b3(1): gis bsdu// dgos pas nges par bstan pa gang // gsang sngags ngo bo gang la gzhag/ snga ma'i don 'di dgongs par gsungs// zhes gsol to// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ dri ba lnga yi
4b4(1): yon tan 'di gsungs so// dang po mdo yi rtsa ba gsum// phyi dang nang dang gsang ba'o// phyi la rtsa ba yan lag gnyis// rtsa ba gzir dang rang gshed dbab// yan lag 'khor lo lo thog gzhom// dregs dgu
4b5(1): gnyis pa'i las su bshad// nang la rtsa ba yan lag gnyis// rtsa ba bzhi dang yan lag drug/ rgyu dang 'khor lo tsit+ta gsang // spogs dang dmar len rtsa bar 'brel// lo zog gzhom dang srog dbrog
4b6(1): gzer// phyag rgyas bsrung dang ltas ngan nad// spyi dril nga gnyis ldan par bshad// gsang skor drag sngags mdo rtsa bzhi// dbang sdud gab don drag po dgu// rtsa ba chen por mdo 'brel ba'o// dbang sdud brgyad
5a1(1): gnyis rtsa ba bzhi// bcu gnyis thun mong sbyor bar bshad// gab don rtsa ba yan lag gnyis// rtsa ba drug gi drong don ni// gnyen sreg bsnol mar lto bshad brgyad// rten dang dug mda' las de
5a2(1): bzhin// yan lag srung ba las gnyis ldan// de bzhin bcu drug rdzogs par bshad// mgo dgu'i sbyor ba rnam pa gnyis// rtsa ba dang ni yan lag go/ rtsa ba bzhi gnyis bsad dang gzir// yan lag thun mong
5a3(1): khyad par dang // rtsal 'gran drag pos 'joms pa'o// thun mong sbyor ba drug gnyis ldan/ khyad par rang bshad rgyud dang ldan// kun gyi rjes gcod bzhi ru gsungs// rtsal 'gran bcu gsum de bzhin lnga// de
5a4(1): bzhin lnga bcu gcig tu bshad// drag po mngon phyung sbyor ba lnga yis rdzogs// thun mong sbyor ba de bzhin lnga dang ldan/ khyad par las kyi rim pa de bzhin bzhi// gsang ba'i sbyor ba lnga gnyis yin// yang gsang
5a5(1): sbyor ba rnam gnyis ldan// sbyor ba drug gnyis thabs dang ldan// mchog gi sbyor bsreg pa lnga dang srin mo'i sbyor ba bcu/ snying po don gyi sbyor ba gsum du gnas// thun mong sbyor ba drug po lnga/ khyad par gsum
5a6(1): dang gsang mchog gsum// bcu dang gcig las sum cur 'gyur// de bzhin drag po'i las la drug cu rtsa dgur bshad// dgos pa'i don chen gnyis dang 'brel ba bzhi// mtha' ru bsreg dang 'khor lo mnan
5b1(1): pas bsdu// dgongs pa'i don gsum de bzhin gsum// bgrod pa gsum gsum gsal ba gsum// de bzhin dgongs pa'i 'bras bu gsum// zhing khams khrom tshogs mnyam dgongs nas// don gnyis snang
5b2(1): stong dngos med pa// lung dang man ngag kun dgongs yin// ngo bo chos dang chos can dang // chos nyid dbyer med lhun gyis grub// snang ba sgyu ma lhun grub la// sgyu ma'i bde ba mngon du 'char// chos nyid ye shes
5b3(1): lhun grub la// sna tshogs snang la ngos gzung med// gang mthong de nyid kho na bas// gsang sngags ngo bo de kho na'o// dpal tshe bdag gi dgongs rgyud nag po las// gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// // de nas
5b4(1): bcom ldan 'das kyis 'khor de dag la chos thams cad 'byung ba'i gzhi 'di gsungs so// snang srid 'khor 'das brkam chags chos// rgyu med tshul gyis rkyen dang bral// 'byung ba lnga dang rigs lnga ye shes
5b5(1): la// rang byung 'gag med stong bdag med// rgyu rkyen mi rtog dang las byung // 'dod pa'i rgyun rgyu/ dag rkyen dag stong // don dam chos sku skye med las// spros med don dam snying po nyid// rgyu 'bras ro gcig
5b6(1): mnyam nyid dang // kun gsal 'bras bu don gcig phyir// phyi nang chos kun rgyu rkyen bral// brkam chags sdug bsngal stong bdag med// sdug bsngal nyid na ye shes de// 'gro ba rab grol ye sangs
6a1(1): rgyas// bden gnyis ma rtog stong bdag med// rtsol bsgrub bya byed 'chang ba'i nad// rtsa ba kun 'dus don gcig la// bsgom bsgrub bya rtsol rtsal med rgyan// chos kun skye med snying po rtsal med
6a2(1): pas// nam mkha'i dpe bzhin stong bdag med// skye med nam mkha' rtsol sems bral// don dam chos nyid ma skyes pas// dpe med nam mkha' lta bur bshad// rtsa ba gcig pas thams cad mkhyen// ngo bo med
6a3(1): phyir cir snang srid// ma skyes pas na thams cad 'byung // sangs rgyas sku gsung ye shes zugs// sems can lus ngag bag chags la// snang srid chos rnams kun gyi gzhi// snying po byang chub sems las
6a4(1): byung // sangs rgyas zhing dang pho brang gnas// kun yin gang min rang rig nyid// ye shes thig le gcig la gsal// srid pa gsum du snang ba yang // lam lnga rgyud lnga gnas lnga 'khor// la sogs sdug bsngal
6a5(1): mnyam la sogs// sdug bsngal rtsal med mnyam par gnas// thabs kyi phyag rgyas rang grol ba'o// chos sku skye 'gag med pa las// drag sngags ye shes rol par shes// dpal tshe bdag gi dgongs rgyud nag po
6a6(1): las/ chos nyid kyi don gtan la dbab pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas 'khor gyi dam pa rdo rje snying pos bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang chen po la gsol pa/ rgyud ces bya ba ci ltar lags// 'khor
6b1(1): lo zhes bya ji ltar dbye// tshe srog bdag po'i don gang lags// sbyor ba'i rim pas las gang byed// gsang sngags ngo bor gang gis btags// zhes gsol to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dri ba lnga'i don
6b2(1): rgyas par bshad do// rgyud ces bya ba gsum yin te// gzhi dang lam dang 'bras bu'i rgyud// lta spyod 'khor lo dbang dam tshig/ lam gyi rim pa sbyor ba'i tshad// ngo bo 'brel bcas rgyu dang rkyen// phyi dang nang dang
6b3(1): gsang ba ste// rang bzhin gnas pa mngon byed pa'i// thabs kyi rgyud ni gsum dang ldan// de mtshon mngon pas rgud ces bya// 'khor lo zhes su bstan pa yang // rten 'brel bsam gtan gzugs brtan
6b4(1): sngags// sreg byed mnan pa ye shes rig/ de yi rim pa rgyas pa na// snang srid phyi nang 'khor ba'i chos// rten 'brel bcu gnyis tshul gyis ni// rten 'brel srid pa'i 'khor lo bshad// rang lus brtan pa'i sku
6b5(1): nyid gsal// spyi bo mgrin pa snying lte ba// gsang ba rjes 'jug rten drug na// se ru sum cu gnyis bcu drug/ brgyad dbus dngas ma drug cu bzhi// bzhi bcu drug dang ldan par gnas// yon tan drag sngags du
6b6(1): mas mdzes// ha dang oM dang e dang A// raM yaM dbus na rkyen dang sdud// srog shing si ra dri dang rgyu// de bgrod phyag rgya chos skur gsal// bsam gtan gnas pa'i 'khor lor bshad// gzugs brnyan 'khor lo
7a1(1): dur khrod kyi// ro ras zhing lpags rgya shog la// sme ba lnga dang rus pa bsku// gang dmigs rten gyi 'khor lo bca'// kha sbyar rus sbal phag mo'i lhor// bcas la gzugs brnyan 'khor long
7a2(1): bshad// gcod pa sngags kyi 'khor lo ni// mtshon cha'i 'khor lo me dang 'dra// srog gzugs rtsa gcod bag chags bsreg/ g.yon skor log nas gcod pa ni// chu yi 'khor lo rlung dang 'dra// skyel zhing ring
7a3(1): dal bla gnas sdud// dbugs kyi rta bskyon rlung gi rkyen// rkyen dang phrad na lte ba 'khor// lte ba'i rkyen gyis rtsibs dag gcod// gcod pa sngags kyi 'khor lor bshad// sreg pa me yi 'khor lo dag/ sa chu dug
7a4(1): gi rten 'brel gyis// sbyor ba kun srog tshe dpal bskyed// zhi rgyas dbang drag lhun gyis grub// mchog tu ma yi 'khor lor bshad// mnan pa 'khor lo las kyi mthar/ kha sbyor pho mo'i thod pa la// rim pa gsum
7a5(1): bri steng dang 'og/ rgya gram gru gsum sbrul dang me// ri rab rus sbal mchod rten gyi// mnan sngags ming rus snying po khams// zod par snying po'i bcud bsdad la// gnad dgu mi nad 'joms dgu yin// mnan
7a6(1): zad pa'i 'khor lor bshad// ye shes rig pa'i 'khor lo yin// thams cad lhun gyi grub pa yi// rol pa ma 'gags cir yang gsal// don gnyis mngon du spyod par byed// rang byung 'khor lo rang rig
7b1(1): pas// ye shes nyi ma'i 'khor lor bshad// de phyir 'khor lo zhes su bshad// tshe srog bdag po gang gsungs pa// snang srid 'khor 'das snang stong gi/ yon tan srog dang sbyor ba'i las// yon tan dbang po che
7b2(1): bkrag kun// 'bru gnyis dag la bsdus nas 'char// skye med rnam dag dbyings su thim// las dang sbyor ba smin zhing rgyas// de phyir tshe srog bdag por bshad// sbyor ba'i rim pas brgya brgyad bcu// che ba'i
7b3(1): yon tan du ma byed// gang brtsams 'bras bu smin zhing rgyas// de phyir sbyor ba'i las su bshad// gsang sngags ngo bo gnyis med las// 'khor ba sgyu ma lhun gyis grub// gzhi rtsa med cing thog mtha'
7b4(1): med// 'das pa'i ye shes lhun gyis grub// gang mthong cing snang byang chub sems// sems phyir ma gsal rang rig pa// bde ba chen por don la thebs// de phyir gsang sngags ngo bor bshad// dpal tshe bdag
7b5(1): gi dgongs rgyud nag po las/ yon tan dris pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis rgyud kyi don gtan la dbab pa 'di gsungs so// de yang rnam pa bdun du dbab// gsum
7b6(1): pa spyod pa'i khyad par ni// bya ba med par kun rdzogs pas// rtsol bral gdeng gsum ldan pa yi// bla dor re dogs med par spyod// sbyor sgrol bya ba gang byas kyang // sems phyir gang yang byas snang med// las
8a1(1): kyi sbyor ba du ma yang // gang ltar byas kyang 'bras bu 'byung // lam gnyis lnga yi sa bgrod kyang // sems dpa'i las su gol pa med// chags sdang lnga yis lam spyad kyang // 'jig rten pa la gzhi
8a2(1): rtsa med// rang bzhin lhun grub spyod pa'i mchog/ dmyal sogs tsha grang kun spyad kyang // 'khor ba nyid na ye shes spyod// lha yi sku dang cha lugs dag/ 'dod dgu lhug par ci spyad kyang // snang stong gnyis med ye
8a3(1): shes sku// gang ltar bltas pa de ltar snang // rtog sgrib skyon yon yongs kyis med// gtub brdung drag po'i spyod pa yang // gar dgu tshul dgu khro bo'i spyod// chos nyid zhe sdang khros pas grol// ye shes nges par
8a4(1): gtan la dbab// rang byung dag pa'i spyod par bshad// dpal tshe bdag gi dgongs rgyud nag po las/ bya ba med pa'i spyod pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis brtul zhugs
8a5(1): bgrod pa'i dbang 'di gsungs so// slob ma dbang gzhan thob pa la// bgrod pa mthar phyin rdzogs pa'i dbang // ngo bo sems kyi chos nyid la// rnam grangs gnyis dang rdzas kyi dbang // rim pa brtul zhugs
8a6(1): rang dbang rdzogs// dper na rgyal po 'phru gu la// rgyal sar ma bton sa mi thob// dbang thob rgyal srid mnga' brnyes tshul// bdag dbang mtshon pa'i rim pa ni// sems nyid dben pa'i bde gnas su// rang
8b1(1): nyams brtan pa'i mtshams bcad nas// maN+Dal chen po'i bya ba brtsam// sngon du 'gro ba'i las rdzogs nas// dur khrod brdal ba'i rgyu blang la// thugs kyi sprul pa mkha' khyab spro// gugs rgyal dri yis khrus byas
8b2(1): la// man+dal dbus su brtan par bzhag/ bsam gtan bum pas rten sbyangs la// lus la gshin rje'i dkyil 'khor brtag/ tsit+ta 'od kyi pho brang du// tshe srog bdag po'i dkyil 'khor brtan// brtan pa rnyed phyir
8b3(1): tshogs gtor la// bya ba'i rim pa bsgrub pa brtsal// brtul zhugs rim pa'i rten du bzhag/ mtshan ldan bkra shis gzungs ma 'dam// rgyal rigs rje rigs sngags skyes ma// mkha' khyab rdo rje mdas ma
8b4(1): reg/ lus dang yan lag dbang po 'jam// ske ring phra 'jam tshigs mig zlum// dpral ba'i dbyes che smin dkyus ring // mig phra dkyil nag ut+pal mdog/ shes rab spyod pa'i rnal 'byor ldan// lus la lha yi
8b5(1): dkyil 'khor brtag/ tsit+tar rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor brtag/ b+ha ga gsang ba'i pho brang du// lhun gyis grub pa'i dkyil 'khor brtag/ bde ba chen po'i rten du gzung // rdo rje gsang ba'i chu rgyun gyis// dkyil
8b6(1): 'khor lnga dang slob ma bkru// gsang ba lhun gyis grub pa yi// dkyil 'khor lha la gsol ba gdab// byin rlabs brtul zhugs 'jug pa brtsam// yol bas par bcad me tog ldan// sdig pa bshags dang
9a1(1): sdom pa dbog/ dam tshig bsgrags la me tog dor// dkyil 'khor lha yi rnam pa bstan// lce la bdud rtsi lung bstan bzhag/ bu de brgyan zhing phyag rgya bsgom// tshogs la rol la lha ngo
9a2(1): bstan// rdzas dang dkyil 'khor byin gyis brlab// slob ma gzhug phyir gsol ba gdab// lhun grub rang bzhin gnas pa'i pho brang nas// ye shes rgya mtsho lhun gyis grub pa'i lha// ma lus mnyam pa'i rgyal po
9a3(1): dgongs su gsol// slob ma mtshan ldan yum gyi dkyil 'khor du// brtul zhugs drag po'i stobs kyi gzhug tu gsol// bde chen mnyam pa'i pho brang gsang ba ru// rig pa brtul zhugs stobs kyis gzhug tu
9a4(1): gsol// slob mas me tog thogs la brda' phyag btsal la gsol ba gdab bo// ston pa'i sgron ma bcom ldan 'das// lha dang slob dpon dgongs su gsol// dregs pa stobs kyi tshul bstan pa// 'gyur med
9a5(1): bde chen pho brang nas// dregs pa'i lha tshogs dgongs su gsol// b+ha ga gsang ba'i pho brang nas// mnyam pa'i rgyal po dgongs su gsol// dam tshig dka' thub sdom pa'i mchog/ rig pa'i rgyal po bdag la
9a6(1): stsol// gsang ba'i ye shes bdag la stsol// ye shes rol pa bdag la stsol// me tog rin chen dmigs dbyig kyang bsdus la// bde chen phyi yi 'jug pa brtsam// phung po lha yi dkyil 'khor bstan// bam
9b1(1): chen thugs kyi dkyil 'khor dum bstan// 'jug pa nang gi lha ngo bstan// gzungs ma lus kyi dkyil 'khor du// gsang ba phyi yi lha ngo bstan// tsit+ta nang gi lha ngo bstan// b+ha ga gsang ba'i pho brang du// gdong
9b2(1): g.yogs dang ldan spro ba bskyed// bkra shis mtshan ldan gsang ba'i pho brang du// gnyis med sangs rgyas nyid dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// byang chub sems nyid mi 'gyur bde ba'i mchog/ pho brang lhun gyis grub par
9b3(1): bzhugs pa dang // sme ba lnga dang bdud rtsir sbyor ba'i sems// bkra shis mtshan ldan bde ba'i brtul zhugs sbyin// mi 'gyur brtan pa'i sku dang ye shes bgrod// de nas gsang ba'i gzungs ma spro ba bskyed par
9b4(1): bya'o// ho// bde chen gsang ba'i pho brang du// thabs chen gsang ba'i bde phab nas// dbu ma'i rtsa brgyad sa bon bsreg/ b+ha ga'i gnas su chos skur bsgril// rtsa lam 'od 'phros longs spyod sku// mnyam par
9b5(1): gnas pa byang chub sku// spros bral kun khyab sprul pa'i sku// brtan pa thob pa rdo rje'i sku// yab yum mnyes pas mnyes par bya'o// de nas gsang ba sbyor ba'i brdas// ye shes nyi zla'i thig le yi// bde bas gang
9b6(1): bar byas pa la// sbyor ba dag pa'i byin rlabs las// rtsa rgyud bde phab thig le bsgril// byang chub sems dang sme ba bsre// bkra shis mtshan ldan bum par bskyil// brtul zhugs rab 'byams dbang bskur
10a1(1): bya// ho// rig pa'i stobs ldan sbyor ba'i gnas// 'khrul pa'i bag chag sprin lta bu// ye shes rol pa'i sgron ma gsal// mnyam pa'i shugs kyi brtul zhugs longs// e ka ya ma pra tIts+tsha ho// me
10a2(1): tog dor la mgo la gdags// mtshan ldan bkra shis pho brang dang // drag po stobs kyis lha ngo bstan// bkra shis bum pas dbang bskur bya// ho// ye shes lhun grub bum pa yis// brtul zhugs dag pa'i dbang
10a3(1): bskur bas// 'gro ba rnam dag chos skur gsal// rang byung ye shes dbang thob shog/ e ka ya ma gu h+ya b+ha ga bo d+hi tsit+ta ho// 'bras bu khrag 'thung ye shes lngar// rdzogs pa'i phyag rgyar lhun grub pa'o// de nas
10a4(1): dur khrod rgyan gyi dbang sbyin pa ni/ glang chen stag sham zhing lpags sbrul// thod pa'i snying phreng keng rus brgyan// me ri dur khrod dbang bskur bas// dregs pa'i stobs dang ldan par shog/ e ka ya ma ha sti//
10a5(1): ma hA nA ga ka pa laM/ tsit+ta dza la ni ri ho// de nas phyag mtshan sbyin pa ni// ho// 'khor ba 'dral byed 'khor lo dang // nyon mongs gcod pa'i ral gri dang // chos nyid mtshon pa'i rdo rje yis// sku gsum mnyam pa'i
10a6(1): dbang thob shog/ e ka ya ma tsakra khaD+ga badz+ra ho// be con dug lnga ye shes lnga ru sgrol// gtun shing gdug pa gnas su 'joms// sdigs mdzub dug gsum sku gsum ngang du rdzogs// rig pa stobs kyi sgo gsum
10b1(1): dbang thob shog/ e ka ya ma b+hi ha hu ti sa ra pa ho// mnyam pa'i brtul zhugs sbyin pa ni// ho// rdo rje pad+ma mnyam sbyar nas// pad+ma rak+ta byang chub sems// bam chen sme ba don dang sbyar// brtul zhugs rol pa'i
10b2(1): dbang bskur bas// mi zad rgyan gyi dbang thob shog/ e ka ya ma gu h+ya rak+ta// bo d+hi tsit+ta ho// mAM sa rak+ta tsit+ta ho/ pU dza kai ni ri ti ho// dpa' brtul sngags kyis byin bskyed pa'i// bam chen ro la mnyam par
10b3(1): rol// rdo rje brjid pa'i dbang thob nas// bde chen mnyam nyid thob par shog/ e ka ya ma a d+hi pa ta sid+d+hi ho// longs spyod rdzogs pa'i dbang bskur bya// 'chi med rang byung ra sA yan// bkra shis mtshan ldan
10b4(1): lhag pa'i rdzas// 'phel 'grib med pa'i dbang bskur bas// rigs lnga ye shes lnga yi dbang thob shog/ e ka ya ma sarba pany+tsa a mr-i ta/ dz+nyA na shud+d+ha ho// bkra shis dngos grub ga'u ru// mi 'gyur brtan pa'i
10b5(1): tshe bsgril nas// rang rtags tshe yi dbang bskur bas// 'chi med rtag pa'i dbang thob shog/ e ka ya ma A yur+d+ha na sid+d+hi ho// snod kyi 'jig rten gtor gzhong du// bcud kyi sems can gtor mar
10b6(1): gsal// 'byung ba rnam lnga gtor ma'i rgyu// lhun grub kun 'byung gtor ma'i rgyan// 'dzin chags med pa'i stobs kyis rol// e ka ya ma ma hA ba lin+ta pU dza ho// dam tshig bsgrags la mna' chu blud par
11a1(1): bya'o// snod med brtul zhugs zhan pa la// spel zhing bsgrags na rdo rje khro bo dang // gtum po gnod sbyin rdo rje dbang chen gyis// lus khral mgo gshag tsiN+Da khrag tu 'thung // e ka ya ma kA ya wA ka
11a2(1): tsit+ta rak+ta khA hi ho/ khyod kyi rdo rje 'chang chen nga yin pas// bka' yi zur yang bcag par bya ba min// bsgo ba byos la dam tshig srog ltar srung // gal te 'das na rdo rje dmyal bar lhung // e ka ya ma dun ra ka
11a3(1): ho// 'di ni rdo rje dmyal ba'i chu// tshul 'di bsrungs na dngos grub thob// nyams na tsit+ta gshag ste 'pho// rdo rje'i chu 'di khyod kyis longs// badz+ra kro d+ha e dam ho// 'dod pa lnga yi tshogs la rol// rgud gsum
11a4(1): lhag pa'i man ngag bstan// rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gral thob yin// brtul zhugs gsang ba'i bgrod pa gsum// thob na mi ldogs la gnas// brtul zhugs gsang ba'i dbang du bshad// dpal tshe bdag gi
11a5(1): dgongs rgyud nag po las/ brtul zhugs dbang gi le'u ste lnga pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dam tshig gzungs kyi don 'di gsungs so// de dag rgyas pa 'di lta ste// dka' thub dam tshig sdom
11a6(1): pa'i mdo// chos rnams ma lus byang chub sems// 'khor 'das lhun grub ngang du 'dus// de mtshon dam tshig srog ltar bsrung // dam tshig rnam pa gnyis yin te// thun mong khyad par rim par gsungs// thun
11b1(1): mong rtsa ba yan lag gnyis// sku gsung thugs dang bco lnga yis// bsdus te bsrung mtshams shes pa'o// khyad par kho na dka' thub dang // bsrung ba bcu gnyis gcig tu gsungs// gsang ba'i lam ni rtogs pas
11b2(1): lam mi bzur// drag sngags thun mtshams khri bar gtam mi bya// 'jig rten pa dang dman la phyag mi btsal/ khro bo'i chas dgu gar dgu gsal bar brtag/ mtshan ldan gzungs ma blang dor med par spyad// rdo
11b3(1): rje'i ra ba'i rdzing ni mi bshig mngon du spyad// re dogs som nyi med par gzir zhig gzhom// tsha ba gsum dang rul gsum myang bar spyad// 'khor lo gzir mtha' sbyin bsreg mnan pa zor// lus kyi dbang po
11b4(1): gzhan gyis mthong mi bya// shes rab spyod pas bla ma'i zur mi bcag/ khyad par dag las kho na'i dka' thub bshad// sprul pa'i khyad par dam tshig bsrung bar gsungs// rdo rje'i rmang gi ri mi bshig/ mngon
11b5(1): 'byung brtul zhugs dogs med spyad// gcan gzan rgyal po gsad mi bya// za ma tog tu dug mi blug/ rin chen lha brag bran yang bsreg mi bya// gangs kyi zhun chu btung ba min// bdud rtsi snod ngan nang mi
11b6(1): blug/ mi shis snod du mdangs mi dbab// snod ngan seng ge'i zho mi blug/ yid bzhin nor bu bsreg mi bya// bya khyung gshog pa bcag pa min// gnam lcags ur mo nang mi 'thab// stag gzig rol pa'i lhag
12a1(1): mi btung // rdo rjes gtam pa'i brag mi bshig/ rdo rje'i ra ba'i rmang mi 'dral// mun pa sel ba'i sgron mi gsad// rdo rje chu bo'i rka mi gcad// rgyal po'i phyag rgya'i rtags mi dbyi// rdo rje'i rdzong gi
12a2(1): brag mi bshig/ rin chen rgyal mtshal rtse mi dbrog/ lhag pa'i dam tshig bsrung bar bshad// brtul zhugs lam las cig car bgrod// 'bras bu bgrod thob lhun gyis grub// las dang sbyor ba kun dang
12a3(1): ldan// mthu stobs byin rlabs shugs kyis 'byung // dam can rgya mtsho der gnas 'grub// de ma yin na mdze dang g.yan// dus min tshe zad mnar med 'pho// legs nyes bgrod med gnyis gar byed// bsrung

12b2(1): gtso// srin mo kha 'dar khrag skyug gtso// rtsub 'khor srog bcad yak+Sha'i gtso// zhe sdang gdug pa sbrul mgo'i gtso// dregs pa bco brgyad / bgegs rigs stong phrag brgyad cu'i gtso// de yi bdag po

16a1(1): 'bras g.yo// he sa 'bru brgyad thun mong gnon// he sa ya ma thi sa ra ya sa nA ga snying gzer sbyar nan rbad/ sman dang 'phye bo rlung sgor 'jug/ mdze rlung khrag sgre tsha grang 'khrugs// bcu gcig pa yi
16a2(1): sngags kyis gnon// sa nA ga srog la dun dun rbad// sa nA ga tsarbad thum ril shag/ sa nA ga rtsa rbad thum ril shag/ sa nA ga dun ling thum ril shag/ sa nA ga srog la hur thum ri la shag/ sa nA ga snying gzer
16a3(1): spusbusgur nan thum ril shag/ sa nA ga du me ma ma srog gzir rbad thum ril shag/ sa nA ga tsa tri shu la gzir nan thum ril shag/ sa nA ga nr-i tri yaM shig gzir thum ril shag/ rkang gcig pu ga rtsa gnyis
